 The comments apane rajya ke logon se mulaakaat karne haridwar pahunche chouhan ne kaha, "jab aap prakruti ke saath chhedchhad karenge to prakruti apana kahar aap par dhayegi
 " uttarakhand main nadiyon ke kinare khadey ho rahe bhawanon par unhone kaha, "gaiyrkanoonee nirmaan or bhrashtachar saath-saath chalate hai
 " negi ne kaha, "kunjwaal ne ek anumaanit sankhya di he
 This is an estimate at the moment
 sankhya isse kam ho sakati he yaa isse bad sakati he
 It is too early to tell the exact number of people killed in the disaster that completely devastated the state
 " unhone kaha yah akalan sarkari karmchaariyon or raahat dal dwaara bachaae gaye logon kii sankhya par aadhaarit he
 Meanwhile, Bahuguna has reported the number of people missing in the flood
 bahuguna ne kaha, "rajya main or duusari jagahon par gumshudagi kii darj karai gai reporton ko dhyaan main rakhte hue mujhe bataaya gaya he ki jo log laapata hai unki sankhya kareeb 3000 he
 "he said that the close of all the missing people have been instructed to report the case to the authorities
 mukhyamantri ne kaha, "laapata logon ke ashrith yadi hamen shapathpatr denge to ham unhen muaavje kii puri raashi denge
 " uttarakhand main 14 june se teen dinon tak baari barish or badal fatne se baadh aa gai or bhuskhalan hue jisase sainkadon logon kii maut ho gai, jabaki sainkadon ab tak laapata hai
 More than 100,000 people have so far been evacuated from the affected areas, while hundreds are still stranded
 jahaan 300 se 400 log abhi bhi badrinaath ilaake main fanse hue hai or raahat kii pratiksha kar rahe hai, vahiin sainkadon bharvahak or 2000 se zyada tattuon kaa kahin koi ata-pataa nahin he
 The NGO has claimed that some of them have been washed away or trapped in the inundation, which need to be removed without delay, otherwise they will die of hunger
 kedarnath main 5 se 10 feet neeche keechad or malbe main kai shav dabe hone se mahamari failane kaa khatra mandara rahaa he
 Health Minister Negi said, "our first priority is to dig out the dead bodies
 duusari praathamikta kedarnath ghati ke sampurna maarg ko behaal karnaa he
 The third priority is to see that there are no epidemics
 ham sthiti par najar rakhe hue hai
 There is nothing to fear yet
 " In order to complete the process quickly, the state government has asked the Center for digging machines
 iske alaava rajya sarkaar ne aapadaa main maare gaye pashuon ke avshesh nipataane ke liye centre se 100 ton bleaching powder kii bhi maang kii he
 Negi said, "with the help of humans, it is not possible to excavate dead bodies
 hamane centre sarkaar se aisi mashine bhejne ke liye kaha he
 Machines can be dropped from the airways and with their help we will be able to excavate the dead bodies by digging in the Kedarnath valley
 " Kedarnath, the center of faith of crores of Hindus from India and abroad, is situated in the lap of the Himalayas on the banks of the Mandakini River at an elevation of 3586 meters above sea level
 yahaan tak 14 kilometre pahari rasta paar kar pahunchaa ja saktaa he

 unhone uttarakhand kii aapadaa ko rashtriya aapadaa ghoshit karne kii bhi maang kii he

 " uttarakhand main nadiyon ke kinare khadey ho rahe bhawanon par unhone kaha, "gaiyrkanoonee nirmaan or bhrashtachar saath-saath chalate hai
 " is bich bahuguna ne sailaab main laapata logon kii sankhya 3000 bataai he

 " unhone kaha ki sabhi laapata logon ke karibiyon ko maamle kii report adhikariyon ko dene kaa nirdesh diya gaya he
 The Chief Minister said, "if the dependents of the missing people give us the affidavit, then we will give them the full amount of compensation
 " Heavy rain and cloudburst triggered floods and landslides in Uttarakhand for three days from June 14, killing hundreds of people, while hundreds are still missing
 prabhavit ilaakon se abhi tak lagbhag 100,000 se zyada logon ko nikaala ja chukaa he, jabaki sainkadon abhi bhi fanse hue hai

 enjio ne daawa kiya he ki inamen kuch sailaab main bah gaye yaa phir fanse hue hai jinhen avilamb nikaale jane kii jarurat he nahin to ve bhukh se mar jaaenge

 teesri praathamikta yah dekhnaa he ki koi mahamari nahin faile
 We are monitoring the situation
 abhi tak dar kii koi baat nahin he
 " prakriya ko sheeghra puri karne ke liye rajya sarkaar ne centre se jameen khodne vaali mashine maangi he

" " a day after the Allahabad High Court canceled the acquisition of nearly 600 acres of land in Greater Noida, the builders affected by the incident met officials of the Greater Noida Authority to resolve the deadlock and find solutions
 greater noida audyogic vikaas praadhikaran ne bilderon ko apni samasyaon or maangon ke saath ek gyaapan saunpane ko kaha

" ek anya real estate company supertech ke nideshak mohit aroda ne kaha ki praadhikaran ke adhikariyon ne hamen aashwaasan diya he ki ve noida ekstansion main kisaanon ke saath sampark main hai or jald hi koi samaadhaan nikaal liya jayega
 On Tuesday, Allahabad High Court awarded 589 in Patwari and Devla villages
 13 hectare bhoomi kaa adhigrahan radd kar diya
 In these villages falling in Dadri tehsil of Gautam Budh Nagar district, this land was acquired by the Greater Noida Authority
 iske baad, real estate companiyon ke sheersh nikaay cridai ne kaha tha ki vah hoicourt ke nirnay ko supreme court main chunauti degaa
 The decision of the High Court will affect more than 20,000 customers and 11 projects of various developers including Amrapali, Supertech, Panchsheel, Arihant and Nirala
 madhya pradesh ke mukhyamantri shivaraj singh chouhan ne vyaapman ghotaale kii jaanch sibiai se karaane ko lekar hoicourt main arji dene kii baat kii he, lekin congress mahasachiv digvijay singh sirf isse santusht nahin hai
 They demand that the CBI be investigated, but under the supervision of the Supreme Court
 gyaat he ki is babat unki yachika par supreme court 9 july ko sunwaayee honi he
 Digvijay spoke to NDTV India immediately after Shivraj's move and said, 'it is good that God has given Shivraj Singh goodwill
 ' digvijay ne tanj main yah baat kahi he, lekin yah sadabuddhi se zyada vyaapman se jude logon kii ek ke baad ho rahi rahasyamayi mauton ke baad is maamle ke tool pakadaney or supreme court main sunwaayee kii tarikh tay hone se bane dabaav kaa nateeja he
 Shivraj was not ready to hand over the investigation of the Vyapam scam to the CBI till yesterday

 Gumnami Baba breathed his last at Ram Bhawan built in Civil Lines of Faizabad city
 unki maut ke do din baad jab sevakon ne ghar kii talaashi lee to pehali baar ek afvaah faijabad se baahar nikal kar desh ke kone-kone tak ja pahunchi
 In fact, when the baggage in many boxes was taken out, a sudden discussion started that Gumnami Baba was none other than Netaji Subhash Chandra Bose
 ab sawaal ye tha ki agar netaa ji hi gumnami baba the to phir 1945 main vimaan haadase main kiski maut hui thi? kyonki bharat sarkaar tak ye kah chuki thi ki netaa ji kii vimaan haadase main maut ho chuki he
 After all, what was the stuff that Gumnami Baba was telling the leader? So first let's take a look at the baggage recovered from Gumnami Baba's box
 jo saamaan gumnami baba ke paas se mila tha
 It contained photographs of Netaji's birthday celebration celebrated every year on 23 January in Kolkata
 lila roy kii maut par hui shok sabhaaon kii tasviren thi
 There were dozens of round glasses like Netaji
 555 cigarette or videshi sharaab thi
 There were also private photographs of Subhash Chandra Bose's parents and family
 ek rolex kii jeb ghadi thi or azaad hind fuj kii ek uniform thi
 Apart from this, in 1974, the daily Anand Bazar Patrika of Kolkata had news published in 24 installments
 german, japani or angreji sahitya kii dheron kitaaben bhi mili thim
 Commentaries were written on whose pages were found in the indo-china war books
 subhash chandra bose kii mrityu kii jaanch ke liye bane shahanwaaz or khosla ayog kii reportein,saikadon telegram or patr aadi jinhen bhagwanji ke naam par sambodhit kiya gaya tha
 Not only this, maps of the handmade place were also found where Netaji's plane crashed
 azaad hind fuj kii guptchar shakha ke pramukh pavitra mohan roy ke likhe gaye badhai sandesh bhi baraamad hue the
 When all these items were recovered together, slowly the stories of Gumnami Baba started to become famous
 tamaam chashmadid saamne aane lage
 Then an important thing came to know that how could Baba, a common anonymity of North India, speak German, English, Japanese and Bengali so fluently
 or ye sab vahi jubaanen thim, jo netaa ji bolaa karat the
 So now it is decided that the story of Netaji reaching Faizabad should be understood
 aakhir wo yahaan kab, kaise or kahaan se aae?faizabad ke sthaneey logon ke mutabiq gumnami baba yaa bhagawanji 70 ke dashak main vahaan pahunche the
 Initially he used to be a tenant in Lalkothi in Ayodhya
 phir kuch hi din baad basti main jaakar rahane lage
 But the township did not like him very much and Gumnami Baba returned to Ayodhya and stayed at Pandit Ramkishore Panda's house
 phir kuch saal baad unka aglaa padaav tha ayodhya sabji mandi ke bichobich sthit lakhanuwa haata
 Where they stayed in a very secret manner
 aakhri vakt main gumnami baba faijabad ke ram bhawan main do kamare ke makaan main rahete the
 Where he died
 gumnami baba kii maut ke baad saamaan ke saath kuch aisi baaten bhi baahar ain jinako lekar logon ko yakeen sa hone laga tha ki gumnami baba hi netaa ji the
 How to reach Gumnami Baba Faizabad, no one knew from where it came
 gumnami baba hameshaa har jagah behad gupt tareeke se kyon rahete the? gumnami baba kisi ko apana cheharaa kyon nahin dikhaate the? wo koun log the jo har saal 23 janvari or durga puja par gumnami baba se milane gupt tareeke se aate the? 23 janvari netaa ji kaa janm din hota he
 Why are Baba's personal servants not allowed to meet him on these two occasions? If Gumnami Baba was a saint meditating in the jungles, then how did he speak so much frank English and German? Who used to bring famous newspapers, magazines, literature, cigarettes and liquor to Gumnami Baba from all over the world? Why was Gumnami Baba secretly cremated after death? On 9 September 1985, between 9:30 and 10 pm, when Gumnami Baba took his last breath, he was accompanied only by his servant Jagadambay and servant Krishna Gopal Srivastava
 kaha jaataa he ki baba kii maut ke baad unke sevak unki sampatti or viraasat par kabje ko lekar aapas main lard pade or unke kamare par donon ne alag-alag taale laga die
 Baba had 22 big boxes
 jisamen sara saamaan rakhaa tha
 However, during this time the local administration patrolled his house
 aisa daawa kiya jaataa he ki baba ke jivit rahete har 23 janvari ko kolkata se kuch khaas log netaji kaa janmdin manaane unke paas aate the
 But after his death, none of them came to attend Baba's last darshan or to attend the last rites even after his servants sent it to Etilla
 kaha jaataa he ki do din ke intazaar ke baad fouj or prashasan ke aalaa adhikariyon kii maujuudagi main gupachup dhang se gumnami baba ke parthiv sharir ko guftaar ghat le jaakar company garden ke paas antim sanskaar kar diya gaya
 This thing was surprising to the people
 kyonki sainya kshetra main kisi saadhaaran shaks kaa antim sanskaar nahin kiya ja saktaa
 After Gumnami Baba, no one was cremated there again
 aisa aarope he ki antim sanskaar se pehle koi rasayan daal kar unka cheharaa bigaada gaya
 Why this has been done, or even done or not, is not clear yet
 kehete hai jab gumnami baba kii maut ke baad unke netaji hone kii baaten failane lageen to netaji kii bhatiji lalita bose kolkata se faijabad ain or gumnami baba ke kamare se baraamad saamaan dekhakar ye kehete hue fafik padi ki ye sab kuch unke chachaa kaa hi he
 After this, there were demonstrations at several places to investigate Gumnami Baba being Netaji
 jo kaaphi lambey vakt tak chalesarkaar baikfoot par aa gai or is maamle kii jaanch ke liye mukherjee ayog kaa gathan kiya gaya
 However, it could not be proved that Gumnami Baba was the only leader
 iske baad do or kamishan is jaanch ke liye bane lekin sabane gumnami baba ko netaa ji maanane se inkaar kar diya
 Movie Review: Shudh Desi romancedirector: Manish Sharma, Writer: Jaideep sahniactor: Sushant Singh Rajput, Parineeti Chopra, Vani Kapoor, Rishi kapoorduration: 2 hours 13 minutes Four and a half stars out of five
 saal 2013 ko apni desi ghi main paki kabhi imarti si mithi to kabhi bikaaneri seb si tikhi lav story mil gai he
 If there is ever papad belle in life for something that looks like love, then this film is pure desi romance for you
 ek film main jo kuch bhi hona chahie, wo isamen hai
 Great real story, memorable characters, solid acting, foot twitching, and songs that forced Johnny Lever to hum and finally a lesson
 sabak ki pyaar dimagi dhundh ke pare himmat karke jane kaa naam he

 2
 Shuddh Desi Romance is the story of Raghu, a boy who lives in Jaipur and feeds the Firangi, giving momentum to the tourism industry
 raghu kii shaadi ho rahi he tara se, magar ain last main usko kanfusion ho jaataa he

 hamaare aapke jaisaa
